it seems (based on folks sharing incomplete messages when\n50: \t// asking questions, or including extra content that's not part of the\n51: \t// diagnostic) that some readers have trouble easily identifying which\n52: \t// text belongs to the diagnostic and which does not.\n53: \tvar leftRuleLine, leftRuleStart, leftRuleEnd string\n54: \tvar leftRuleWidth int // in visual character cells\n55: \t\t}\n95: \t}\n96: \n97: \t// Before we return, we'll finally add the left rule prefixes to each\n98: \t// line so that the overall message is visually delimited from what's\n99: \t// around it. }\n122: \n123: // DiagnosticPlain is an alternative to Diagnostic which minimises the use of\n124: // virtual terminal formatting sequences.\n125: //\n126: // It is intended for use in automation and VariableValues can potentially contain\\n53: \\t// unknown values for a speculative plan, but the variable values must\\n54: \\t// all be known for a plan that will subsequently be applied.\\n55: \\t//\\n56: \\t// ApplyTimeVariables retains the names of any ephemeral variables that were\\n57: \\t// set (non-null) during the planning phase and must therefore be\\n58: \\t// re-supplied by the caller (potentially with different values) during\\n59: \\t// the apply phase. changes required to move from a current\\n24: // state to a goal state derived from configuration. The described changes\\n25: // are not applied directly, but contain an approximation of the final\\n26: // result that will be completed during apply by resolving any values that\\n27: // cannot be predicted.\\n28: //\\n29: // A plan must always be accompanied by the configuration it was built from,\\n30: // since the plan does not itself include all of the information required to\\n31: // make the changes indicated.\\n32: type Plan struct {\\n33: \\t// Mode is the mode under which this plan was created.\\n34: \\t//\\n35: \\t// This is only recorded to allow for UI differences when presenting plans\\n36: \\t// to the end-user, and so it must not be used to influence apply-time\\n37: \\t// behavior. The actions during apply must be described entirely by\\n38: \\t// the Changes field, regardless of how the plan was created.\\n39: \\t//\\n40: \\t// FIXME: destroy operations still rely on DestroyMode being set, because\\n41: \\t// there is no other source of this information in the plan. New behavior\\n42: \\t// should not be added based on this flag, and changing the flag should be\\n43: \\t// checked carefully against existing destroy behaviors.\\n44: \\tUIMode Mode\\n45: \\n46: \\t// VariableValues, VariableMarks, and ApplyTimeVariables together describe\\n47: \\t// how Terraform should decide the input variable values for the apply\\n48: \\t// phase if this plan is to be applied.\\n49: \\t//\\n50: \\t// VariableValues and VariableMarks describe persisted (non-ephemeral)\\n51: \\t// values that were set as part of the planning options and are to be\\n52: \\t// re-used during the apply phase. VariableValues can potentially contain\\n53: \\t// unknown values for a speculative plan, but the variable values must\\n54: \\t// all be known for a plan that will subsequently be applied.\\n55: \\t//\\n56: \\t// ApplyTimeVariables retains the names of any ephemeral variables that were\\n57: \\t// set (non-null) during the planning phase and must therefore be\\n58: \\t// re-supplied by the caller (potentially with different values) during\\n59: \\t// the apply phase. Ephemeral input variables are intended for populating\\n60: \\t// arguments for other ephemeral objects in the configuration, such as\\n61: \\t// provider configurations. Although the values for these variables can\\n62: \\t// change between plan and apply, their \\\"nullness\\\" may not.\\n63: \\tVariableValues     map[string]DynamicValue\\n64: \\tVariableMarks      map[string][]cty.PathValueMarks\\n65: \\tApplyTimeVariables collections.Set[string]\\n66: \\n67: \\tChanges           *ChangesSrc\\n68: \\tDriftedResources  []*ResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n69: \\tDeferredResources []*DeferredResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n70: \\tTargetAddrs       []addrs.Targetable\\n71: \\tForceReplaceAddrs []addrs.AbsResourceInstance\\n72: \\tBackend           Backend\\n73: \\n74: \\t// Complete is true if Terraform considers this to be a \\\"complete\\\" plan,\\n75: \\t// which is to say that it includes a planned action (even if no-op)\\n76: \\t// for every resource instance object that was mentioned across both\\n77: \\t// the desired state and prior state.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// If Complete is false then the plan might still be applyable (check\\n80: \\t// [Plan.Applyable]) but after applying it the operator should be reminded\\n81: \\t// to plan and apply again to hopefully make more progress towards\\n82: \\t// convergence.\\n83: \\t//\\n84: \\t// For an incomplete plan, other fields of this type may give more context\\n85: \\t// about why the plan is incomplete, which a UI layer could present to\\n86: \\t// the user as part of a warning that the plan is incomplete.\\n87: \\tComplete bool\\n88: \\n89: \\t// Applyable is true if both Terraform was able to create a plan\\n90: \\t// successfully and if the plan calls for making some sort of meaningful\\n91: \\t// change.\\n92: \\t//\\n93: \\t// If [Plan.Errored] is also set then that means the plan is non-applyable\\n94: \\t// due to an error. An errored plan cannot be applied,\\n101: \\t// but can be cautiously inspected for debugging purposes.\\n102: \\tErrored bool\\n103: \\n104: \\t// Checks captures a snapshot of the (probably-incomplete) check results\\n105: \\t// at the end of the planning process.\\n106: \\t//\\n107: \\t// If this plan is applyable (that is, if the planning process completed\\n108: \\t// without errors) then the set of checks here should be complete even\\n109: \\t// though some of them will likely have StatusUnknown where the check\\n110: \\t// condition depends on values we won't know until the apply step.\\n111: \\tChecks *states.CheckResults\\n112: \\n113: \\t// RelevantAttributes is a set of resource instance addresses and\\n114: \\t// attributes that are either directly affected by proposed changes or may\\n115: \\t// have indirectly contributed to them via references in expressions.\\n116: \\t//\\n117: \\t// This is the result of a heuristic and is intended only as a hint to\\n118: \\t// the UI layer in case it wants to emphasize or de-emphasize certain\\n119: \\t// resources. Don't use this to drive any non-cosmetic behavior, especially\\n120: \\t// including anything that would be subject to compatibility constraints.\\n121: \\tRelevantAttributes []globalref.ResourceAttr\\n122: \\n123: \\t// PrevRunState and PriorState both describe the situation that the plan\\n124: \\t// was derived from:\\n125: \\t//\\n126: \\t// PrevRunState is a representation of the outcome of the previous\\n127: \\t// Terraform operation, without any updates from the remote system but\\n128: \\t// potentially including some changes that resulted from state upgrade\\n129: \\t// actions.\\n130: \\t//\\n131: \\t// PriorState is a representation of the current state of remote objects,\\n132: \\t// which will differ from PrevRunState if the \\\"refresh\\\" step returned\\n133: \\t// different data, which might reflect drift.\\n134: \\t//\\n135: \\t// PriorState is the main snapshot we use for actions during apply.\\n136: \\t// PrevRunState is only here so that we can diff PriorState against it in\\n137: \\t// order to report to the user any out-of-band changes we've detected.\\n138: \\tPrevRunState *states.State\\n139: \\tPriorState   *states.State\\n140: \\n141: \\t// ExternalReferences are references that are being made to resources within\\n142: \\t// the plan from external sources.\\n143: \\t//\\n144: \\t// This is never recorded outside of Terraform. It is not written into the\\n145: \\t// binary plan file, and it is not written into the JSON structured outputs.\\n146: \\t// The testing framework never writes the plans out but holds everything in\\n147: \\t// memory as it executes, so there is no need to add any kind of\\n148: \\t// serialization for this field. plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (delete then create):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Read:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# No changes:\\n\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.\n// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tif resource.DeposedKey == \"\" { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones\n\t\t\tchanges[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for consistent output\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := changes[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print action group header\n\t\tswitch action {\n\t\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (delete then create):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (create then delete):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create then forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Read:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# No changes:\\n\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Print each resource\n\t\tfor _, resource := range resources {\n\t\t\tactionSymbol := actionSymbolCompact(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s %s\\n\", actionSymbol, resource.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, resources := range changes {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(resources)\n\t}\n\n\tsummary := formatSummary(counts)\n\tif summary != \"\" {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(summary)\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolCompact returns a short symbol for each action type\nfunc actionSymbolCompact(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"±\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"∓\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"⨥\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \" \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary returns a summary line with change counts\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tif len(counts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tcreates := counts[plans.Create]\n\tupdates := counts[plans.Update]\n\tdeletes := counts[plans.Delete]\n\treplaces := counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]\n\treads := counts[plans.Read]\n\tforgets := counts[plans.Forget] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]\n\n\t// Only show non-zero counts\n\tvar parts []string\n\tif creates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to add\", creates))\n\t}\n\tif updates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to change\", updates))\n\t}\n\tif replaces > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to replace\", replaces))\n\t}\n\tif deletes > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to delete\", deletes))\n\t}\n\tif reads > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to read\", reads))\n\t}\n\tif forgets > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to forget\", forgets))\n\t}\n\n\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %s\\n\", strings.Join(parts, \", (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a string representation of the plan changes in a compact format.\n// It shows one line per resource change and groups changes by action type.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group changes by action\n\tchanges := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, resource := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\tif resource.DeposedKey == states.NotDeposed { // Only include current objects, not deposed ones\n\t\t\tchanges[resource.Action] = append(changes[resource.Action], resource)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order of actions for consistent output\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.NoOp,\n\t}\n\n\t// Output changes grouped by action\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := changes[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Print action group header\n\t\tswitch action {\n\t\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Update:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Delete:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (delete then create):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Replace (create then delete):\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Create then forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Forget:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# Read:\\n\")\n\t\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"# No changes:\\n\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Print each resource\n\t\tfor _, resource := range resources {\n\t\t\tactionSymbol := actionSymbolCompact(action)\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s %s\\n\", actionSymbol, resource.Addr.String()))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Print summary\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, resources := range changes {\n\t\tcounts[action] = len(resources)\n\t}\n\n\tsummary := formatSummary(counts)\n\tif summary != \"\" {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(summary)\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// actionSymbolCompact returns a short symbol for each action type\nfunc actionSymbolCompact(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"±\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"∓\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"⨥\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \" \"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatSummary returns a summary line with change counts\nfunc formatSummary(counts map[plans.Action]int) string {\n\tif len(counts) == 0 {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tcreates := counts[plans.Create]\n\tupdates := counts[plans.Update]\n\tdeletes := counts[plans.Delete]\n\treplaces := counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate] + counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]\n\treads := counts[plans.Read]\n\tforgets := counts[plans.Forget] + counts[plans.CreateThenForget]\n\n\t// Only show non-zero counts\n\tvar parts []string\n\tif creates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to add\", creates))\n\t}\n\tif updates > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to change\", updates))\n\t}\n\tif replaces > 0 {\n\t\tparts = append(parts, fmt.Sprintf(\"%d to replace\", replaces))\n\t}\n\tif deletes > 0 {\n\t\tparts
